NOTICE

NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, A. Javeed Basha was born to my parents Mr. A. Saleem Basha and Mrs. S. Waheeda Begum on 24th April 1992.
I State that except my birth certificate wherein the names of my true parents are found all my educational and other records
declare my paternal aunt Mrs. A. Nasima Begum and her husband Mr. R. Abdul Razak as my parents to whom I was given
by way of adoption and a deed of adoption was executed on 20th March 1998 and the same was registered as Document
No. 186 of 1998 in book No. IV of the Sub-Registry of Mylapore. It was not published in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette
at that time. Challenging the same I filed O.S. No. 549/2013 on the file of the VII Assistant Judge City Civil Court at Chennai
and the Hon’ble VII Assistant Judge City Civil Court at Chennai was pleased to order the suit on 31st July 2013 declaring
that the adoption deed dated 20th March 1998 is null and void. Therefore in furtherance my name should be called
as S. Javeed Basha, son of Mr. A. Saleem Basha residing at No. 8/2, 2nd Street, Narayanaswamy Garden, Greenways
Road, R.A. Puram, Chennai-600 028.
Chennai,
5th June 2014.

A. JAVEED BASHA,

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
